When you turn on the timer and keep focused till the end of the pomodoro - you get rewarded with a nice red Pomodoro. \r\n\r\nIn other cases, when you get distracted or stop focusing early - you get a green Pomodoro.\r\n\r\nOverall it features: \r\n- tracking a focused activity separately from distracted;\r\n- tracking individual contexts that important for you;\r\n- weekly and monthly statistics for analysis;  \r\n\r\nAll that can help you to develop the following habits to fight procrastination. \r\n- be focused in a context from the beginning to the end of the Pomodoro. Instead of focusing on just turning it on;\r\n- to work on efficiency by striving to increase the number of red tomatoes with respect to green ones;\r\n- be aware of the actual distribution of your time within the important contexts of yours;\r\n\r\n\"The Pomodoro Technique\"¬Æ and \"Pomodoro\"¬Æ are registered trademarks by Francesco Cirillo.
